msg:The room is consistent with the pictures. The Qiantang River is visible from the window. The garden environment is nice. name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Garden Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Family
info:11 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted March 30, 2024
msg:Haining is a place worth visiting, and Haining Qianjiang Junting Hotel is a hotel worth staying in. As soon as we arrived at the lobby, the front desk upgraded us to a river view room with a balcony. It was great. We could watch the Qianjiang tide on the balcony. There was a tide-watching platform on the second floor. After we checked in, we watched the tide on the second-floor tide-watching platform. The tide time on the second day was 1:50 pm. Thanks to the front desk for agreeing to check out at 2 o'clock, we watched the Qianjiang tide again on the balcony of the room. I remembered Bai Juyi's poem: Junting pillow watching the tide head, here, isn't it "Junting pillow watching the tide head"!
Junting Hotel is worthy of being a high-end five-star hotel, with complete facilities, good breakfast, polite and thoughtful service staff, and a large and beautiful garden in the hotel. You can stroll in the garden, and there are even peacocks. It's a beautiful hotel tour. Next time I come to Haining, I will definitely stay at Qianjiang Junting Hotel.

name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Business Suite - River-View
info:Stayed in September 2023
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted October 1, 2023
msg:The hotel was booked to watch the high tide around the 18th day of the eighth ***** month.
The room rate during the Tide Watching Festival is really expensive, the river view suite is 3600+, and it is about 1000+ on normal days. I booked this hotel for the convenience of tide watching. There are tide watching platforms on the second and third floors of the hotel open to guests, and there are very few people compared to the Tide Watching Park (see Figure 5, which is the second-floor platform taken from the room when the tide is coming). If there are elderly people and children who are afraid of sun, rain and crowding, then booking here is still a good choice.
During the Tide Watching Festival, there is only a set meal for Chinese lunch on the second floor, 200 per person, and 158 per person for Western buffet on the first floor.
Facilities: Although the hotel is not new, the overall maintenance is good. Parking is convenient. The buffet breakfast is of normal level. There is basically no children's playground. There are several peacocks in the yard.
Sanitation: There is no problem with the sanitation of the room and public areas.
Environment: The location is very good, and the environment of the Wengjin Line in front of the hotel is very good. It is very comfortable to take a walk when there are few people.
Service: Fruits will be delivered in the afternoon, and the service attitude is very good.
Except for the high prices during special holidays, everything else is OK. The kids like it very much and may come back if they have the chance.

msg:The hotel is right by the river, next to the scenic area, with ample parking lots. The rooms are 30+ square meters, and you can see the river from the window. There are tide-watching platforms on the 2nd and 3rd floors of the hotel, and you can watch the tide directly from the hotel, but the viewing platform is still a distance away from the river, so the sense of participation is definitely not that strong, but there are few people, and this advantage is irreplaceable. It is about 700 to 800 meters away from the Tide-Watching Park, and it takes about 10+ minutes to walk. The green shade along the way is also very pleasant, and you can meet many people walking to the park. The hotel itself feels like it has been around for a while, but the overall maintenance is good, it is also large, there are many rooms, and some rooms have balconies, where you can watch the tide. The overall feeling is very quiet, recommended.
